<h2><span id="English" class="mw-headline">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Edit section: English" href="/w/index.php?title=apple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;" class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright">

<div class="floatnone"><img width="44" height="44" data-file-height="200" data-file-width="200" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" alt="" /></div>

<h3><span id="Etymology" class="mw-headline">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Edit section: Etymology" href="/w/index.php?title=apple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Middle English language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English_language">Middle English</a></span> <i lang="enm" class="Latn mention"><a title="appel" href="/wiki/appel#Middle_English">appel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Old English language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English_language">Old English</a></span> <i lang="ang" class="Latinx mention"><a title="ppel" href="/wiki/%C3%A6ppel#Old_English">ppel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss">apple, any kind of fruit, fruit in general, apple of the eye, ball, anything round, bolus, pill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Proto-Germanic language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i lang="gem-pro" class="Latinx mention"><a title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/aplaz" href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/aplaz">*aplaz</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss">apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Scots language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language">Scots</a></span> <i lang="sco" class="Latn mention"><a title="aipple" href="/wiki/aipple#Scots">aipple</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a title="w:West Frisian language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language">West Frisian</a></span> <i lang="fy" class="Latn mention"><a title="apel" href="/wiki/apel#West_Frisian">apel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Dutch language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language">Dutch</a></span> <i lang="nl" class="Latn mention"><a title="appel" href="/wiki/appel#Dutch">appel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a title="w:German language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language">German</a></span> <i lang="de" class="Latn mention"><a title="Apfel" href="/wiki/Apfel#German">Apfel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Swedish language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language">Swedish</a></span> <i lang="sv" class="Latn mention"><a title="pple" href="/wiki/%C3%A4pple#Swedish">pple</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Proto-Indo-European language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i lang="ine-pro" class="Latinx mention"><a title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/hbl" href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82%C3%A9b%C5%8Dl">*hbl</a></i>, <i lang="ine-pro" class="Latinx mention"><a title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/hbl (page does not exist)" class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82%C3%A9bl%CC%A5&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1">*hbl</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss">apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Irish language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language">Irish</a></span> <i lang="ga" class="Latn mention"><a title="ll" href="/wiki/%C3%BAll#Irish">ll</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Lithuanian language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i lang="lt" class="Latn mention"><a title="obuolys" href="/wiki/obuolys#Lithuanian">buols</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Russian language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language">Russian</a></span> <i lang="ru" class="Cyrl mention"><a title="" href="/wiki/%D1%8F%D0%B1%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%BA%D0%BE#Russian"></a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jbloko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly <span class="etyl"><a title="w:Ancient Greek language" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek_language">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i lang="grc" class="polytonic mention"><a title="" href="/wiki/%E1%BC%84%CE%BC%CF%80%CE%B5%CE%BB%CE%BF%CF%82#Ancient_Greek"></a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mpelos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss">vine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span id="Pronunciation" class="mw-headline">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Edit section: Pronunciation" href="/w/index.php?title=apple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a title="w:American English" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English">US</a><span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> <a title="w:British English" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English">UK</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a title="Appendix:English pronunciation" href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">p()l</span>, <a title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet" href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a title="Appendix:English pronunciation" href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span lang="" class="IPA">/.pl/</span>, <span lang="" class="IPA">[.pl]</span></li>

<h3><span id="Noun" class="mw-headline">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Edit section: Noun" href="/w/index.php?title=apple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong lang="en" class="Latn headword">apple</strong> (<i>plural</i> <span class="form-of lang-en plural-form-of"><b lang="en" class="Latn"><a title="apples" href="/wiki/apples#English">apples</a></b></span>)</p>
<ol>
<li>A <a title="common" href="/wiki/common">common</a>, <a title="round" href="/wiki/round">round</a> <a title="fruit" href="/wiki/fruit">fruit</a> produced by the <a title="tree" href="/wiki/tree">tree</a> <i><a title="Malus domestica" href="/wiki/Malus_domestica">Malus domestica</a></i>, cultivated in <a title="temperate" href="/wiki/temperate">temperate</a> climates. <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span>
<span class="HQToggle">[<a href="javascript:(function(){})()">quotations</a>]</span><ul style="display: none;">
<li><b>c. 1378</b>, <a title="wikipedia:William Langland" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Langland">William Langland</a>, <i><a title="wikipedia:Piers Plowman" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Piers_Plowman">Piers Plowman</a></i>:
<dl>
<dd>I prayed pieres to pulle adown an <b>apple</b>.</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1815</b>,  <a title="wikipedia:Jane Austen" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jane_Austen">Jane Austen</a>,  <cite>Emma</cite>:</span>
<dl>
<dd><span class="cited-passage">Not that I had any doubt before  I have so often heard Mr. Woodhouse recommend a baked <b>apple</b>.</span></dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
<li><b>2013</b>, John Vallins, <i>The Guardian</i>, 28 Oct 2013:
<dl>
<dd>Close by and under cover, I watched the juicing process. <b>Apples</b> were washed, then tipped, stalks and all, into the crusher and reduced to pulp.</dd>
</dl>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Any of various tree-borne <a title="fruit" href="/wiki/fruit">fruits</a> or <a title="vegetable" href="/wiki/vegetable">vegetables</a> especially considered as resembling an apple; also (with qualifying words) used to form the names of other specific fruits such as <i lang="en" class="Latn mention"><a title="custard apple" href="/wiki/custard_apple#English">custard apple</a></i>, <i lang="en" class="Latn mention"><a title="thorn apple" href="/wiki/thorn_apple#English">thorn apple</a></i> etc. <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span>
<span class="HQToggle">[<a href="javascript:(function(){})()">quotations</a>]</span><ul style="display: none;">
<li><b>1658</b>, trans. Giambattista della Porta, <i>Natural Magick</i>, I.16:
<dl>
<dd>In Persia there grows a deadly tree, whose <b>Apples</b> are Poison, and present death.</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li><b>1784</b>, <a title="wikipedia:James Cook" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Cook">James Cook</a>, <i>A Voyage to the Pacific Ocean</i>, II:
<dl>
<dd>Otaheite [] is remarkable for producing great quantities of that delicious fruit we called <b>apples</b>, which are found in none of the others, except Eimeo.</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li><b>1825</b>, Theodric Romeyn Beck, <i>Elements of Medical Jurisprudence</i>, 2nd edition, page 565:
<dl>
<dd><i>Hippomane mancinella.</i> (Manchineel-tree.) Dr. Peysonnel relates that a soldier, who was a slave with the Turks, eat some of the <b>apples</b> of this tree, and was soon seized with a swelling and pain of the abdomen.</dd>
</dl>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a title="fruit" href="/wiki/fruit">fruit</a> of the <a title="Tree of Knowledge (page does not exist)" class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Tree_of_Knowledge&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1">Tree of Knowledge</a>, eaten by Adam and Eve according to post-Biblical Christian tradition; the <a title="forbidden fruit" href="/wiki/forbidden_fruit">forbidden fruit</a>. <span class="defdate">[from 11th c.]</span>
<span class="HQToggle">[<a href="javascript:(function(){})()">quotations</a>]</span><ul style="display: none;">
<li><b>1667</b>, <a title="wikipedia:John Milton" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton">John Milton</a>, <i>Paradise Lost</i>, Book X:
<dl>
<dd>Him by fraud I have seduced / From his Creator; and, the more to encrease / Your wonder, with an <b>apple</b> [].</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1985</b>,  <a title="wikipedia:Barry Reckord" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barry_Reckord">Barry Reckord</a>,  <cite>The White Witch</cite>:</span>
<dl>
<dd><span class="cited-passage">Woman ate the <b>apple</b>, and discovered sex, and lost all shame, and lift up her figleaf, and she must suffer the pains of hell. Monthly.</span></dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A <a title="tree" href="/wiki/tree">tree</a> of the genus <i><a title="Malus" href="/wiki/Malus">Malus</a></i>, especially one cultivated for its edible fruit; the <a title="apple tree" href="/wiki/apple_tree">apple tree</a>. <span class="defdate">[from 15th c.]</span>
<span class="HQToggle">[<a href="javascript:(function(){})()">quotations</a>]</span><ul style="display: none;">
<li>
<div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  John Weathers,  <cite>Commercial Gardening</cite>, page 38:</span>
<dl>
<dd><span class="cited-passage">If the grafted portion of an <b>Apple</b> or other tree were examined after one hundred years, the old cut surfaces would still be present, for mature or ripened wood, being dead, never unites.</span></dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
<li><b>2000</b> PA Thomas, <i>Trees: Their Natural History</i>, page 227:
<dl>
<dd>This allows a weak plant to benefit from the strong roots of another, or a vigorous tree (such as an <b>apple</b>) to be kept small by growing on 'dwarfing rootstock'.</dd>
</dl>
</li>
<li>
<div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  Sid Gardner,  <cite>The Faults of the Owens Valley</cite>, <small><a title="w:International Standard Book Number" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number">ISBN</a> <a title="Special:BookSources/9781440177927" href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9781440177927">9781440177927</a></small>, <a href="http://books.google.com/books?id=gcbQzBOnc0YC&amp;pg=PA34&amp;dq=%22watered+the+apples%22" class="external text" rel="nofollow">page 34</a>:</span>
<dl>
<dd><span class="cited-passage">Used to be apple orchards, used to be the river and irrigation ditches that watered the <b>apples</b>, used to be mining towns.</span></dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
<li>
<div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b>,  Terri Reid,  <cite>The Everything Guide to Living Off the Grid</cite>, page 77:</span>
<dl>
<dd><span class="cited-passage">Other fruit trees, like <b>apples</b>, need well-drained soil.</span></dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a title="wood" href="/wiki/wood">wood</a> of the <a title="apple tree" href="/wiki/apple_tree">apple tree</a>. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the <a title="plural" href="/wiki/plural">plural</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a title="Cockney rhyming slang" href="/wiki/Cockney_rhyming_slang">Cockney rhyming slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Short for <b><a title="apples and pears" href="/wiki/apples_and_pears">apples and pears</a></b>, slang for <a title="stairs" href="/wiki/stairs">stairs</a>. <span class="defdate">[from 20th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">baseball<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a title="Appendix:Glossary" href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang">slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a title="Appendix:Glossary" href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a title="ball" href="/wiki/ball">ball</a> in baseball. <span class="defdate">[from 20th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a title="Appendix:Glossary" href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> When smiling, the round, fleshy part of the cheeks between the eyes and the corners of the mouth.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a title="pejorative" href="/wiki/pejorative">pejorative</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a title="ethnic" href="/wiki/ethnic">ethnic</a> <a title="slur" href="/wiki/slur">slur</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a title="Native American" href="/wiki/Native_American">Native American</a> or red-skinned person who acts and/or thinks like a <a title="white" href="/wiki/white">white</a> (<a title="Caucasian" href="/wiki/Caucasian">Caucasian</a>) person.
<span class="HQToggle">[<a href="javascript:(function(){})()">quotations</a>]</span><ul style="display: none;">
<li>

W. Norton &amp; Company, <small><a title="w:International Standard Book Number" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number">ISBN</a> <a title="Special:BookSources/0393045579" href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0393045579">0393045579</a></small>, <a href="https://books.google.com/books?id=ztCBIMWqtLUC&amp;pg=PA537&amp;dq=apple" class="external text" rel="nofollow">page 537</a>:</span>
<dl>
<dd><span class="cited-passage">The presenter, close to tears, told the audience that she's really an <b>apple</b>white on the inside and red on the outsideNative American.</span></dd>
</dl>
</div>
</li>
<li>
<div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> November 12,  Joel Spring,  <cite>The Cultural Transformation of A Native American Family and Its Tribe 1763-1995: A Basket of <b>Apples</b></cite><sup><a href="https://books.google.com/books?id=APEvisJqs1oC&amp;pg=PT245&amp;dq=apple" class="external autonumber" rel="nofollow">[1]</a></sup>, Routledge, <small><a title="w:International Standard Book Number" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number">ISBN</a> <a title="Special:BookSources/1136494715" href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/1136494715">1136494715</a></small>, ch. 9:</span>
